##########
#  German Defeat - Soviets in Berlin - SOV annexes Germany
##########
event = {
	id = 131301
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = {
		event = { id = 131300 days = 1 }
		OR = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			NOT = {
				exists = GER
			}
		}
		control = { province = 300 data = SOV } #Soviets in Berlin
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131301_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131301_DESC"

	#picture = ""

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131301_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		#command = { type = inherit which = GER }
		#command = { type = sleepevent which = 131301 } #SOV annexes Germany
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131302 } #USA annexes Germany
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131303 } #UK annexes Germany
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131304 } #Unknown annexes Germany
	}
}

event = {
	id = 131304
	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = {
		atwar = yes
		NOT = {
			event = 131300 #Fall of the Third Reich
			control = { province = 300 data = GER } #Berlin lost
			control = { province = 300 data = SOV } #No Soviets in Berlin
			control = { province = 300 data = USA } #No Americans in Berlin
			control = { province = 300 data = ENG } #No Brits in Berlin
			control = { province = 175 data = GER } #Moscow lost
			control = { province = 212 data = GER } #Minsk lost
			control = { province = 238 data = GER } #Kiev lost
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
			war = { country = SOV country = ENG }
			war = { country = ENG country = USA }
		}
		lost_national = { country = GER value = 97 }
	}

	#date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1940 }
	#offset = 3
	#deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131304_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131304_DESC"

	#picture = ""

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131304_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131301 } #SOV annexes Germany

	}
}

	desc = "EVT_131331_DESC"	#第二次大戦の終結とともに、フランスは連合軍軍政地域の中に自国の領域を作り、自国の保護領とした。フランスはザールをドイツから分離するために様々な手を尽くし米英はこれを承認したが、1945年にはソ連に反対されたこと、1955年にはザールの住民自身がドイツへの合流を望んだことにより成立することはなかった。

		command = { trigger = { country = SOV } type = setflag which = SOV_admits_French_Saal }

	}

	id = 131384
	random = no
	country = USA

	trigger = {
		puppet = { country = DFR country = USA } # DFR isn't ENGpuppet
		NOT = { exists = DDR }
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
			war = { country = SOV country = ENG }
			war = { country = ENG country = USA }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			#event = 131303
			event = 131304

	}
